RJE'I GSHED KYI BKA' SDONG RJE BLA MA'I BKA' SRUNGS YIN, NGED

RNAMS KYIS RJE BLA MA'I BSTAN BA SRUNG ZHING RJE BLA MA'I BSTAN

YIN GSUNG NGO, ,KHYAD BAR CHOS RGYAL NANG SGRUB MA HE'I GDONG PA
CAN BZHIS

BSKOR BA BYON NAS, KHO BO NI GSHIN RJE GSHED KYIS RJE BLA MA'I
BKA' BSRUNGS SU BKA' BSGOS BA YIN, KHYOD RNAMS KYIS BDAG LA YID
BRTAN PAR BYOS SHIG ,BDAG GIS KYANG RJE BLA MA'I BSTAN

PA SRUNG BA YIN ZHES GSUNG ZHING PHYI SGRUB KYIS DBYUG TO PHYAG
TU GTANG BYUNG NGO, ,SKU TSE SNGA MA GCIG LA RGYAL BA MA PHAM PA
BYON NAS, LHO 'DZAM BU GLING DU STON PA DNGOS DANG KHYAD PAR MA
MCHIS PA'I SH'AKYA

DE'I
